SELECT * FROM `vax_data` WHERE `recvdate` = '2021-01-01' AND `state` = '934906' AND `age` = '18'
###[ List all the records where they took their shot in 934906 and they are 18 years old and they have a history of diabetes. ]
Answer:
SELECT * FROM `vax_data` WHERE `recvdate` = '2021-01-01' AND `state` = '934906"

3931,"SELECT * FROM `vax_adverse_events` WHERE `RECVDATE` = '2015-12-04'
###[ Find all the records where the adverse event started on 12/04/2015 and the patient is female. ]
Answer:
